	# map_patronizing_colonizers
	PC_HOSTILE_GREETING_01 = {
		weight = {
			weight = 3
		}
		trigger = {
			has_ai_personality = map_patronizing_colonizers
			NOT = { is_at_war_with = FROM }
			OR = {
				is_hostile_to = FROM
				is_unfriendly_to = FROM
			}
		}

		weight = {
			weight = 3
		}
		trigger = {
			has_ai_personality = map_civilized_nomads
			NOT = { is_at_war_with = FROM }
